<div id="review_1022505685" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1022505685" />
    <a title="Merelee Knott" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33040106-merelee-knott"><img alt="Merelee Knott" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1405300543p2/33040106.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1022505685?book_show_action=true">Aug 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Merelee Knott" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Merelee Knott" href="/user/show/33040106-merelee-knott">Merelee Knott</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1022505685" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4852822748114907730">One of the books I love to read and re-read again, and again, and again! You have to be patient in the beginning. The second time around, it's hilarious right from the start. The hero's sister and brother-in-law describe him as having no initiative, no fun, and he'll never go anywhere. They are so wrong! Long before the end, he has travelled halfway around the world. Not an easy feat for a nearly peniless, happily married, stay-at-home, Englishman in that era. Historical fiction authors take not</span>
  <span id="freeText4852822748114907730" style="display:none">One of the books I love to read and re-read again, and again, and again! You have to be patient in the beginning. The second time around, it's hilarious right from the start. The hero's sister and brother-in-law describe him as having no initiative, no fun, and he'll never go anywhere. They are so wrong! Long before the end, he has travelled halfway around the world. Not an easy feat for a nearly peniless, happily married, stay-at-home, Englishman in that era. Historical fiction authors take note. This writer's settings and cultures are spot-on ... because he was writing about his own time. (It's an old book.) Imagine a world when only the very rich could travel, when very few people had ever flown in an airplane, when there were no satellites to show you the weather before you decided to travel across the Pacific in a very small sailboat. Romance authors, take note. This story includes a rollicking funny romance, too! General fiction authors take note: characters grow and change in the best stories. Personally, I cheat. I use teenage heros. It's easy to clobber a teen with life and get him to change. Neville Shute takes a middle-aged man very set in his ways -- and hits him hard enough to force change. This author expose a very couragous character in the process. If you like strong characters, or funny characters, or machinery, or sailboats, or airplanes, or romance, or historical fiction, I think you'll love Trustee From the Toolroom.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4852822748114907730" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NZtqlDD/c9P3dWw9EAq72pSJDDZ/+2W71zQl8KgqI7lzf6mrjhZPpCZek6OjOI8TnZtN45o5fDP2vMJpjklbLg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IdmwTfsRiNKeKSqhtXS0fDnhg4LugyYe1QSe7JxNsB5nPXNyRfi0pU8C1T8GRoC1MPPCVwtBP5b0jHl1ui7IiQ==')})
  }

All for expressing a personal opinion rooted in faith, in response to a completely hypothetical question. A new front in the culture war had been opened.  When the owners of the pizza parlor told Dana Loesch on a Blaze TV interview that they might never reopen, Loesch started a fundraising campaign. The people donating weren’t taking a stand against gay rights; they just believed that a random mom-and-pop shop shouldn’t be run out of business because media and political elites on both coasts caricature and vilify rural Americans. Most of the problems with our country today can be traced to a very simple cause – the growing disconnect between the government and media elites and the rest of us, the old-fashioned, hard-working, God-fearing Americans who are proud to live in middle America.       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/21477.Nevil_Shute">About Nevil Shute</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/21477.Nevil_Shute"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1547804311p3/21477.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/21477.Nevil_Shute">Nevil Shute
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
599
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer12084721724669724469">Nevil Shute Norway was a popular British novelist and a successful aeronautical engineer. <br/><br/>He used Nevil Shute as his pen name, and his full name in his engineering career, in order to protect his engineering career from any potential negative publicity in connection with his novels. <br/><br/>He lived in Australia for the ten years before his death.</span>

</div>
</div>
